UKR_Lend_leas1_category = {
	UKR_order_weapons_in_Ukraine = {
		icon = decision_category_generic_arms_trade
		fire_only_once = yes
		available = {
			has_completed_focus = UKR_large_batch_of_small_arms
		}
		#  visible = {
		#     UKR_can_sell_weapons_trigger = yes
		# }
		days_remove = 2
		cost = 9
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				has_equipment = {
					infantry_equipment < 1
				}
				factor = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_manpower < 10000
				factor = 0				#need to up conscription laws
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			UKR = {
				add_offsite_building = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment_2
				amount = 50000
			}
		}
	}
	UKR_order_ammo_in_Ukraine = {
		icon = decision_category_generic_arms_trade
		days_remove = 30
		cost = 9
		fire_only_once = no
		available = {
			has_completed_focus = UKR_large_batch_of_small_arms
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = UKR_nato_have_ammo
				#Высчитываем, сколько место осталось у Украины на складах
				set_temp_variable = {
					ammo_needed = ammunition_free_space
				}
				#Ограничиваем максимумом в 200к
				clamp_temp_variable = {
					var = ammo_needed
					min = 0
					max = 200
				}
				NTO = {
					check_variable = {
						ammunition_variable > ammo_needed
					}
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = UKR_nato_have_enough_ammo
				NTO = {
					check_variable = {
						ammunition_variable > 200
					}
				}
			}
		}
		#  visible = {
		#     UKR_can_sell_weapons_trigger = yes
		# }
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				has_equipment = {
					infantry_equipment < 1
				}
				factor = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_manpower < 10000
				factor = 0				#need to up conscription laws
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
		}
		remove_effect = {
			#Высчитываем, сколько место осталось у Украины на складах
			set_temp_variable = {
				ammo_needed = ammunition_free_space
			}
			#Ограничиваем максимумом в 200к
			clamp_temp_variable = {
				var = ammo_needed
				min = 0
				max = 200
			}
			#Передаём боеприпасы
			add_to_variable = {
				ammunition_variable = ammo_needed
			}
			NTO = {
				subtract_from_variable = {
					ammunition_variable = ammo_needed
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_ammo_supply_from_nato_tt
		}
	}

UKR_information_war = {
	UKR_discrediting_government_Russia = {
		icon = UKR_discrediting_Russia
		fire_only_once = no
		days_re_enable = 20
		cost = 25
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 15
		}
		available = {
			original_tag = UKR
		}
		visible = {
			original_tag = UKR
		}
		complete_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
				var = global.rus_information_war_var_sum
				value = -2
				tooltip = IW_2_rus_minus_var_add_tt
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_to_variable = {	
					var = global.ukr_information_war_var_sum
					value = 2
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { global.rus_information_war_var_sum > 100 }
					}
					set_variable = {	
						var = global.rus_information_war_var_sum
						value = 100
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { global.ukr_information_war_var_sum > 100 }
					}
					set_variable = {	
						var = global.ukr_information_war_var_sum
						value = 100
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { global.rus_information_war_var_sum < 0 }
					}
					set_variable = {	
						var = global.rus_information_war_var_sum
						value = 0
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { global.ukr_information_war_var_sum < 0 }
					}
					set_variable = {	
						var = global.ukr_information_war_var_sum
						value = 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
